    FROM [Claims] AS [c]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [c].[UserId] = [a].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN [Departments] AS [d] ON [c].[DepartmentId] = [d].[DepartmentId]

) AS [t]

    FROM [ApprovalLogs] AS [a0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a1] ON [a0].[ApproverId] = [a1].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ClaimId] = [t0].[ClaimId]
